 a 90-minute special session on the Mumbai Stock Exchange (BSE) was conducted to examine the software to deal with the disaster
 vishesh satr bisai or neshnal stock exange (enesai) donon main yojit kiya gaya
 On this day, a 90-minute special session at the Mumbai Stock Exchange (BSE) for most brokerage companies and foreign institutional investors was held to examine the software to deal with the disaster
 vishesh satr bisai or neshnal stock exange (enesai) donon main yojit kiya gaya
 On this day, large-scale trading was not seen in the stock markets due to lack of working days for most brokerage companies and foreign institutional investors

 ' Kapil Mishra, the minister of the Aam Aadmi Party government, has written a blog to talk about treating rapists like terrorists
 kapil mishra ne blog main likhaa he ki balaatkaari, kisi aatankwaadi se kam nahin he or inhen mrityudand milanaa hi chahie
 Kapil Mishra wrote, 'in a year, 450 minor girls were raped in Delhi alone
 aadha desh lagaataar is dar main ji rahaa he
 In Jobulandshahr, Huawo can happen to anyone at any time, and the worst thing is that hearing such incidents does not make us hurt anymore
 'kapil mishra ne blog ke jariye chaar badi baton kaa zikr kiya he-1
 Whatever the age of the rapist, there must be punishment
 agar tumhaari umr balaatkaar karne laayak he, to tum uski sajaa kaatane laayak bhi ho
 No sympathy should be given in this
 2
 If we cannot protect women, let them protect themselves
 sabhi ladakiyon ke haath main hathiyaar dekar, prashikshan do
 Let them kill those who want to rape them
 3
 Punish them harshly but quickly and harshly
 jaise ki sansad ko bulandshahr cond ke liye ek vishesh kanoon laana chahie or balaatkaariyon ko saarvajanik rup se maaraa jaae
 So that everyone knows what happens to those who hand over their daughters and sisters
 4
 The identity of the rapist and the victim should be made public so that everyone knows them
 agar koi pita yaa ankal he
 
 
 Those who have sexually harassed our little girls, then everyone should know their name and address
 ye abhi hoga yaa kabhi nahinam aadmi partybanane se pehle nirbhaya andolan kaa hissaa rahe kapil mishra blog me likhte hai, 'hamaari betiyaan or bahanen jo lagaataar dar main ji rahi hai, unhen bhi har din pratadit kiya ja rahaa he
 She is facing a war like every day
 hamen ise ek ladaai ghoshit kar dena chahie or yuddh jaise hi ladanaa chahie
 Usually i am against the death penalty but i would like to say that the scammers are terrorists and they should be treated like them
 ' The Greek team, which won the Euro 2004 Championship, registered their first win in the World Cup finals by defeating 10-player Nigeria 2-1 in a thrilling Group b match here today
 is jeet se yunaan kaa vishwa cap kaa sapana ab bhi barkaraar he
 In the 1994 Finals, the team had to face defeat in all three matches and then now South Korea defeated them 2-0 in the first match here
 unhen pataa tha ki is mukaable ko ganvaana unhen dakshin africa se baahar kaa rasta dikhaa saktaa he
 But Dimitrios Salfingidis scored the 44th and Vasilios Torasidis scored the winning goal in the 71st minute
 vahiin nyeegeria ko group bi ke apane pehle match main argentina se 0-1 se haar mili thi
 For him, midfielder Kalu Uche gave the team the lead in the 16th minute but they could not keep it up
 is haar ke baavjood super eagles kii team aankadon ke hisaab se nakout charan main pahunch sakati he
 Ten players Nigeria and Greece were 1-1 up until half time
 lekin vasilios torasidis ne 71wein minute main ribound par gol daaga

 shrikrishna janmashtami par aapaki har manokamana puri ho sakati he
 Worshiping Shri Krishna on Janmashtami brings children
 yahi nahin pujan karne vaale jataka ko dderghaayu kaa vardaan miltaa he or samruddhi kii prapti hoti he
 People who have weak moon can benefit from special worship on Janmashtami
 shrikrishna janmashtamiutsav hamen apane puure parivaar ke saath anand se manaanaa chahie
 After bathing in the morning and cleaning the house, the idol of Laddu Gopal should be installed on a silver or wooden slab
 kaisaa ho shringaar- shri krishna ko shringaar behad pasand he
 Therefore, you should adorn them with great love on their birthday
 shringaar main phulon kaa khub prayog karen
 - Especially make them wear yellow clothes, gopi sandal and sandal fragrance
 - shri krishna ke shringaar main is baat kaa dhyaan rakhen ki vastra se lekar gahanon tak kuch bhi kaala nahin hona chahie
 Do not use black at all
 - vaise to aap shri krishna par pile phool chadha sakate hai
 But it would be best if the flowers of Vyjayanthi are offered to Krishna ji
 kya hoga inkaa prasadjanmashtamike din log kanha ko kai tarah ke pakwaan chadhaate hai
 Some even make a modern-day breakfast for them
 lekin, janmdiwas ke din shri krishna ko aisi chijen chadhaanaa sarvottam hoga, jo kanha ko pasand he
 Offer these things to Lord Krishna on Janmashtami
 
 
 1
 Offer Panchamrit, also add basil in it
 2
 Meva, Makhan and Misri are very dear to Krishna
 isliye inkaa bhoga bhi lagaaein
 3
 kahin-kahin, dhaniye kii panjiri bhi arpit kii jaati he
 4
 purna satvik bhojan, jisamen tamaam tarah ke vyanjan hon, is din shri krishna ko arpit kiye jate hai
 How to celebrate Janmashtami- Take bath early in the morning and resolve to fast or worship on Janmashtami
 dinabhar jalaahar yaa falahar grahan karen, satvik rahen- madhyaraatri ko bhagwaan krishna kii dhaatu kii pratimaa ko kisi paatr main rakkhen
 - Bath that statue first with milk, then with curd, then with honey, then with sugar and finally with ghee
 - isi ko panchamrita snaan kehete hai, iske baad jal se snaan karaaen
 - Then offer Pitambar, flowers and Prasad - Keep in mind that the things offered will be offered only by putting in the conch - the person worshiping will not wear black or white clothes - then chant the mantra according to your wish - Finally Receive and distribute offerings 'khamoshiyaan'film ne gharelu box offis par 'hawaijada' or 'rahasy' se behatar kamai kii he

 - taran adarsh (@taran_adarsh) February 2, 2015 Know how the film 'khamoshiyan' - Input IANS rashtrapita mahatma gandhi kii pratimaa landan ke parliament square main lagegi
 The announcement has been made by British Foreign Minister William Hague and the then Finance Minister George Osborne

 While the hair does not dry quickly in this season, there is a bad smell from the hair which is wet for a long time
 baalo se aane vaali gandh bahut tej hoti he
 Actually, this smell is due to moisture
 bal dhone ke baad jab wo bahut der tak geele rah jate hai to unamem badboo aane lagati he
 If the moisture in the hair remains for a long time, it also increases the risk of fungal infection
 fungal infections kii vajah se baalo kii jaden kamjor ho jaati hai or bal jhadanaa shuru ho jate hai
 In such a situation, try not to stop the moisture in the hair
 bal dhone ke baad jitani jaldi ho sake baalo ko sukha len
 Follow these steps to remove the problem of smelly hair: 1
 baalo kodhote samay scalp bhi acchhee tarah safakaren
 Use anti-fungal or anti-bacterial shampoos to avoid infection
 aap chahen to tulsi kii pattiyon ke pani kaa bhi istemaal kar sakati hai
 2
 apni diet main vitamin si se yukt chizon kaa istemaal karen
 Along with this, include all the nutritious things in the diet that are necessary for health
 3
 If you take too much tea or coffee, then reduce its intake
 bahut adhik maatra main cold drink yaa soft drink lenaa khatarnaak ho saktaa he
 4
 baalo ko bahut der tak geela nahin rahane den
 If you are wet in the rain, dry the hair immediately after reaching home

 It is said that a moment changes the life of a human being and that moment came in the life of Deepa Karmakar, India's 'wonder Girl' in gymnastics, when in 2010, after failing to win a medal, a fellow player gave him a 'buffalo' and his Coach Bishweshwar Nandi was called 'donkey'
 rio olympic main chauthe sthaan par rahakar bhartiya jimnastic kaa sabase sunaharaa adhyay likhane vaali deepa bhale hi padak se maamuli antar se chook gayi, lekin unhone ‘tafarih ke liye toornament main aae’ maane jane vaale jimnaston ko sammaan or padak ummid kaa darja dilaayaa

 unke aansu tham nahin rahe the or aise main ek saathi purush jimnast ne kaha daalaa ,‘yah bhens he or iskaa coach gadhaa
 'this taunt hurt him deep inside and now he had one goal in front of him like Arjuna - winning the medal
 rio main deepa kii kamyaabi sabhi ne dekhi, lekin dilli main mili us taane se rio tak ke safar ke peeche kii unki mehnat or tripura jaise purvottar ke chote se rajya se nikalakar antarrashtriya khel maanchitr par apni pahchaan banane ke unke safar kii gaatha bhi utani hi dilachasp he
 It has been chronicled in 'deepa Karmakar: The Small Wonder'
 apni honhaar shishyaa ko olympic padak pahante dekhne kaa sapana coach nandi kii ankhon main bhi pal rahaa tha
 The taunt found in Delhi gave Deepa sleep, and the game itself hurt her wounds when she won five medals at the 2011 National Games in Ranchi
 iske baavjood unhen pataa tha ki sheersh jimnaston or usamen abhi kaaphi fark he

 khelon main paanch chah maheene hi rah gaye the, lekin deepa ko apni mehnat or coach ke bharose par yakeen tha, lihaaja usne hami bhar di
 There was mixed reaction in team management and among fellow players to do this 'volt of Death'
 deepa ne trial main produnova kiya or pehla test paas kar gai
 She worked six to eight hours every day and finally the day had come, which she was waiting for from the Delhi Commonwealth Games
 scotland main qualifing daur ke liye abhyaas ke dauraan hi unki edi main chot lag gai
 He did all the exercises with the injury
 coach nandi ko laga ki rashtramandal padak jeetne kaa sapana khel shuru hone se pehle hi tut gaya, lekin deepa ne qualifi kiya
 The final was three days later and she could not practice due to injury
 final main dard kii parvaah kiye bina deepa kii nazren sirf padak par thim
 It was not an immediate honor for him, but a way of answering those who were questioning his skill
 yah uske saath uskaa sapana dekh rahe coach nandi ko uski gurudakshina thi
 It was his insistence on honoring Indian gymnasts
 deepa ne glasgo main mahilaon ke volt main kaansya padak jitkar itihaas rach daalaa

 kolkata-kathmando-kolkata udaan kaa saptaah main chaar baar sanchaalan hota he
 The spokesman said that Air India will operate one additional flight each from New Delhi and Kolkata with relief material through scheduled flights

 air india ne teen niyamit sevaaon main se kal ek udaan kaa hi sanchaalan kiya or bukamp aane ke bahut pehle isane udaan bhari thi

30 am

lekar bahut zyada updrav karata he- is mangal ke kaaran aksar vaivaahik jivan main hinsa aa jaati he- par yah mangal sampatti or sampatti sambandhi kaaryon main laabhakaari hota he- vyakti bade pad or dher sari sampattiyon kaa swami hota he- is mangal ke prabhaav ko samaapt karne ke liye mangalvaar kaa upwas rakkhen- ek tambe kaa challa , mangalvaar ko , anamika anguli main dhaaran karengar mangal
